Which means, the narrator instills a tinge of â€œreality will always be harsherâ€ in this line itself, before going onto talk about the uncertainty of the fate of this love story in another line. Despite all the odds stacked against them, these love birds have dared to step out. The once restrained and reserved souls are now flourishing in love for each other, He says.
